<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">Certification &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;53</P>

<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:21.6pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:21.6pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:568.8pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">Page 2</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=center><B>PART I</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM 1. &nbsp;DESCRIPTION OF BUSINESS</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>General Development of Business</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Jewett-Cameron Trading Company Ltd. (the &quot;Company&quot;) was incorporated in British Columbia, Canada, on 7/8/87, as a holding company for Jewett-Cameron Lumber Company (&#147;JCLC&#148;). &nbsp;The Company acquired all of the shares of JCLC through a stock-for-stock exchange and on 7/13/87, Jewett-Cameron Lumber Corporation became a wholly owned subsidiary of Jewett-Cameron Trading Company Ltd.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Jewett-Cameron Lumber Corporation (&quot;JCLC&quot;) was incorporated in the state of Oregon, USA, in September 1953. &nbsp;During the next 31 years it developed a good reputation as a small lumber wholesaler based in Portland, Oregon. &nbsp;In September 1984, the original stockholders sold their interest in the corporation to a new group of investors. &nbsp;Two members of that group remain active in the company: Donald M. Boone and Michael Nasser.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>JCLC acquired Material Supply International (&quot;Material Supply&quot;) in early 1986. &nbsp;MSI-PRO Co. was incorporated in Oregon, USA, in April 1996 as a wholly-owned subsidiary of JCLC and assumed the business of Material Supply. &nbsp;MSI-PRO Co. is engaged in the importation and distribution of pneumatic air tools and industrial clamps. &nbsp;The product line was renamed &quot;MSI-PRO&quot;. &nbsp;Material Supply is presently inactive.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company&#146;s wholly-owned subsidiary, Jewett-Cameron South Pacific Ltd. (&quot;JCSP&quot;) was incorporated in the Kingdom of Tonga in July 1990. &nbsp;The Company has closed its operations in Tonga. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company&#146;s wholly-owned subsidiary, Jewett-Cameron Seed Company (&#147;JCSC&#148;) was incorporated in Oregon, USA in October 2000. This company was formed after the Company acquired certain assets of a company called Agrobiotech Inc. The assets acquired by the Company were located at 31345 N.W. Beach Road in Hillsboro, Oregon. The assets purchased by the Company consisted of thirteen plus acres of land; 105,000 square feet of buildings; rolling stock; and, equipment. &nbsp;This facility was utilized for seed and grain processing, storage and brokerage. &nbsp;JCSC now operates as a seed and grain processing, storage and brokerage business.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company&#146;s wholly-owned subsidiary, Greenwood Products, Inc. was incorporated in Oregon, USA in February 2002. This company was formed after Jewett-Cameron Lumber Company acquired the business and certain assets of Greenwood Forest Products, Inc., of Portland, Oregon. The assets acquired consisted of nearly $7 million of inventory (at year end) which is scheduled to be purchased in eight installments over a two year period beginning in February 2002 for a price equal to the seller&#146;s cost plus 2%. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 3</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Associated furnishings, equipment and supplies were also purchased for $260 thousand. The Company also purchased a license to use all of the intangible assets of the seller for a five year term, with an option to purchase for a nominal amount at the end of the term, is being acquired for $1 thousand which was paid upon closing. The initial acquisition price was paid from the working capital of Jewett-Cameron Trading Company Ltd. and management expects to purchase the inventory utilizing capital provided by working capital and working capital loans. Greenwood Products, Inc. is continuing the business of Greenwood Forest Products, Inc. This business involves the processing and distribution of industrial wood and other specialty building products, principally to original equipment manufacturers. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>Financial Information About Business Segments</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;United States Dollars</P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 4</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:8pt; font-size:8pt; color:#000000" align=justify>(1)$14,671,878 is attributable to home improvement products and $25,561,159 is attributable to Greenwood Products, Inc.</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>Narrative Description of Business</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The following material describes the business of each of the operating subsidiaries. &nbsp;The holding company and the operating subsidiaries employ a total of 70 people.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U>Jewett-Cameron Lumber Corporation</U></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>JCLC operates out of facilities located in North Plains, Oregon, and Ogden, Utah. The Company competes in the following business segments: warehouse distribution and direct sales of building materials to home improvement centers primarily in the Pacific and Rocky Mountain regions of the United States; export of finished building materials to overseas customers, primarily in central and south America; and specialty wood products for government and industrial sales, primarily on a contract-bid basis.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>During Fiscal 2002/2001/2000, sales of Greenwood Products, Inc. combined with sales to home improvement centers represented about 92.2%/87.6%/95.3% of revenue; with export, industrial tools and seed processing and sales representing 7.8%/12.4%/4.7%, respectively. &nbsp;The Fiscal 2002 decrease in the percent related to export, industrial tools and seed processing and sales is a result of the increased revenues from the first partial year of operations which include the Company&#146;s wholly-owned subsidiary, Greenwood Products, Inc.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>JCLC concentrates a portion of its sales efforts on the home improvement industry, an industry that has not been subject to major business cycles. &nbsp;Traditionally, the new home construction portion of the lumber industry is highly sensitive to the US economy and interest rates and generally suffers during periods of economic decline and high interest rates, due to the reduction in housing starts. &nbsp;JCLC has concentrated on building a customer base in the residential repair and remodeling segment of the industry (a growing market fueled by professional remodelers and do-it-yourself homeowners), making it less susceptible to swings in housing starts.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The products JCLC sells are not unique and with few exceptions are available from multiple suppliers; however, the service provided by JCLC is unique in that it includes bar coding of all products; shrink wrapping of all individual orders; and, just in time delivery to most customers. Export sales are primarily timbers.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">Page 5</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">JCLC's current product categories include:</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* Fencing - A mix of widths, heights, textures, species,</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;prefabricated panels, split rail, and pickets that</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are appropriate for the home improvement centers.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A similar array of posts, post caps, and rails.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:8pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* Residential Decking - A selection of widths, lengths, species,</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;treated and stained products along with</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;accessories such as railings and step</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;risers.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:8pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* Lattice - Stained, painted, and natural panels as well as a</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;selection of vinyl panels.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:8pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* Garden Timbers - Treated, untreated, or stained including</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cherrytone garden ties, bender board, stakes,</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and lath.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Gates</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Arbors</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Pine shelving and furring.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Fire retardant dimension lumber and plywood.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Dimension lumber.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Plywoods and oriented strand board.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Dowels</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Kennels</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Greenhouses</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Portable storage buildings</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">* &nbsp;Outdoor seating</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>A company-owned distribution center and headquarters office facility in North Plains, Oregon was completed in November 1995. &nbsp;This complex includes 40,000 square feet under roof of warehouse, office, and manufacturing space on five paved acres. &nbsp;This facility gives JCLC the capacity to provide a broad range of products and services to its customer base from Northern California to Alaska.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The company also owns a distribution complex in Ogden, Utah, with a 25,000 square foot warehouse and 3,500 square feet of office space on a total of 30 acres. &nbsp;This facility services customers in the Rocky Mountain Region including the states of Utah, Colorado, Wyoming, Montana, Idaho, and northern Nevada.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Inventories are maintained at these facilities and shipped to home improvement center customers. &nbsp;During the season's peak, some of the material is also shipped directly from the producing mill to the customer; as a result, JCLC sells both out of its warehouse facilities and mill direct.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>No patents, trademarks, licenses, franchises, or concessions are held by JCLC and as a result they are not factors in its business.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 6</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Historically, JCLC receives commitments from a number of large home improvement chains in the late fall/early winter to supply product at a fixed price for a specified period of time; i.e., for three months of firm pricing once the season begins.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>

</TD><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=138><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=right>3%</P>
</TD><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=121.2><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=right>13%</P>
</TD></TR>
<TR><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=235.2><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>U.S. Marine</P>
</TD><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=144><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=right>7%</P>
</TD><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=138><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=right>N/A</P>
</TD><TD style="padding-left:7.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:7.2pt; padding-bottom:0pt" align=left valign=top width=121.2><P style="margin:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=right>N/A</P>
</TD></TR>
</TABLE>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The home improvement business is seasonal, with most sales occurring between February and August. &nbsp;Historically, the Company negotiates an agreement with each of its major home center customers in the fall of each year to include products to be carried and approximate volumes required for the coming home improvement season. &nbsp;Deliveries for the new season normally begin in late February, depending on weather.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>JCLC begins buying inventory for the next home improvement season in late fall each year. &nbsp;Consequently, an inventory buildup occurs until the heavy selling season begins in February. &nbsp;Inventory continues to remain high for a few months and then gradually declines to seasonal low levels at the end of the summer.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Backlog orders are not a factor in JCLC's business. &nbsp;No material portions of the business are subject to renegotiation of profits or termination of contracts or subcontracts at the election of the government.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The home improvement center industry is highly competitive. &nbsp;Many of JCLC's primary competitors are much better financed and have sophisticated national distribution networks. &nbsp;These competitors include: (1) Georgia-Pacific, headquartered in Atlanta, Georgia, with distribution centers throughout the service area; (2) Weyerhaeuser, headquartered in Tacoma, Washington, with distribution centers throughout the service area; (3) Boise Cascade, headquartered in Boise, Idaho, with several distribution centers in the service area; and (4) OREPAC Building Products, headquartered in Wilsonville, Oregon, with several distribution centers in the service area. &nbsp;These competitors, particularly Georgia Pacific, Weyerhaeuser, and Boise Cascade, have product lines which are substantially broader than those of JCLC, and therefore reference to their annual sales includes many more product lines than those sold by JCLC.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 7</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>JCLC's home improvement center market area consists of stores in Alaska, northern California, Oregon, and Washington being served out of the North Plains, Oregon warehouse, and Utah, Colorado, Idaho, Wyoming, Montana, and northern Nevada served out of the Ogden, Utah warehouse. &nbsp;Its home improvement sales of $15 million represents less than 1% of the lumber category sales by the major home improvement center chains in this primary service area.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The larger companies are often unwilling to compete with a JCLC or OREPAC in terms of product flexibility and service of individual retail stores. &nbsp;OREPAC, like JCLC, serves the Pacific region; however, their product mix is different and they concentrate on building materials other than lumber and plywood.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>During the spring of 1993, JCLC acquired a manufacturing plant to produce several lines of products for home improvement center customers. &nbsp;The plant was moved to a larger facility in Portland in August 1993, and subsequently was moved to an existing building on the North Plains facility in March 1995. &nbsp;The plant currently custom cuts cedar fencing products and pine boards.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U>MSI-PRO Co</U>.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>MSI-PRO operates from the same facilities as JCLC. MSI-PRO imports and distributes both pneumatic air tools and industrial clamps. &nbsp;Distribution is throughout the United States and Canada to distributors and original equipment manufacturer customers. &nbsp;Sales are made through a network of agents and representatives, each of whom is an independent contractor representing between 10-to-15 other manufacturers who sell to similar customers but are not selling competing lines. &nbsp;MSI-PRO has agents and representatives that cover major industry groupings including industrial suppliers, automotive suppliers, and woodworking suppliers.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The pneumatic air tools, manufactured and sold under the name MSI-PRO, are of a light industrial application and are moderately priced. &nbsp;MSI-PRO exclusively markets the MSI-PRO line.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The industrial clamps are somewhat newer to the Company. &nbsp;The line is high-quality and moderately priced and covers a wide variety of potential customers.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The products have been manufactured for MSI-PRO by several suppliers in Taiwan and South Korea. &nbsp;All products are covered by more than one supplier.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Sales of pneumatic air tools and industrial clamps are not seasonal.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 8</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>MSI-PRO is a registered trademark in the United States and Canada. &nbsp;No other patents, licenses, franchises, or concessions are held by the Company. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The market for pneumatic air tools is very competitive. &nbsp;MSI-PRO faces competition from better financed companies with more sophisticated sales forces and distribution networks. The U.S. market for pneumatic air tools is currently approximately $1 billion in annual sales, of which 60% are manufactured in the United States and 40% are imported. &nbsp;The major US manufactured lines are Chicago Pneumatic and Ingersoll-Rand, which rank #1 and #2 in overall size in the industry. &nbsp;A smaller line, Sioux, is also manufactured in the United States. &nbsp;The two largest imported lines today are Florida Pneumatic and Astro Tools. &nbsp;Others include Sunnex, Ames, and Eagle. &nbsp;MSI-PRO's volume today is a very small fraction of the market. &nbsp;The current market strategy that allows MSI-PRO to compete in the pneumatic air tool and industrial clamp markets includes brand name and company recognition, moderate to low price, and continued development of a manufacturer representative organization which covers all of the major users of the tools.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The U.S. sales volume in industrial clamps is approximately US$400 million annually. &nbsp;There are fewer competitive lines available and MSI-PRO expects to gain a larger share of the market in industrial clamps than in pneumatic air tools.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>There are no customers that purchase 10% or more of MSI-PRO's products in any one year. &nbsp;Backlog orders are not a major factor. No portion of the business is subject to renegotiation of profits or termination of contracts or subcontracts at the election of the government.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U>Jewett-Cameron South Pacific Ltd.</U></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>This Tongan corporation, JCSP, until Fiscal 1999, consisted of three retail building material yards located on separate islands of the Kingdom of Tonga. &nbsp;Products sold included finished lumber, plywood, hardboard, cement, roofing, rebar, windows, doors, plumbing fixtures, floor tile, and other miscellaneous building materials. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In Fiscal 1999 the Company made the decision to wind down its operations in Tonga. As of August 31, 2001, the company had no remaining interests in Tonga.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 9</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>Business Risks</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>This annual report includes &#147;forward&#150;looking statements&#148; as that term is defined in Section 21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. <P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Demand for company products may change;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Production time and the overall cost of products could increase if any of the primary suppliers are lost or if any primary supplier increased the prices of products;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Fluctuations in quarterly and annual operating results may make it difficult to predict future performance;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Shareholders could experience significant dilution;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company could lose its significant customers;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company could experience delays in the delivery of its products;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>A loss of the bank credit agreement could impact future liquidity;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:54pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:486pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The limited daily trading volume of the Company&#146;s common stock could make it difficult for investors to purchase additional shares or sell currently held shares.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>Demand for Company products may change:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In the past the Company has experienced decreasing annual sales in the areas of home improvement products and industrial tools. The reasons for this can be generally attributed to worldwide economic conditions, specifically those pertaining to lumber prices; demand for industrial tools; and, consumer interest rates. If economic conditions continue to worsen or if consumer preferences change, the Company could experience a significant decrease in profitability.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>Production time and the overall cost of products could increase if any of the primary suppliers are lost or if a primary supplier increased the prices of raw materials:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page &nbsp;10</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company&#146;s manufacturing operation, which consists of cutting fencing material to specific sizes and shapes, depends upon obtaining adequate supplies of lumber on a timely basis. The results of operations could be adversely affected if adequate supplies of raw materials cannot be obtained in a timely manner or if the costs of lumber increased significantly.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>Fluctuations in quarterly and annual operating results may make it difficult to predict future performance:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Quarterly and annual operating results could fluctuate in the future due to a variety of factors, some of which are beyond management&#146;s control. As a result of quarterly fluctuations, it is important to realize quarter-to-quarter comparisons of operating results are not necessarily meaningful and should not be relied upon as indicators of future performance.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>Shareholders could experience significant dilution:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company is authorized to issue up to 10,000,000 shares of preferred stock, without par value per share. &nbsp;As of the date of this Annual Report, no shares of preferred stock have been issued. &nbsp;The Company&#146;s preferred stock may bear such rights and preferences, including dividend and liquidation preferences, as the board of Directors may fix and determine from time to time. &nbsp;Any such preferences may operate to the detriment of the rights of the holders of the Common Stock and would cause dilution to these shareholders.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>The Company could lose its significant customers:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The top ten customers of the Company represent 49% of its business. &nbsp;The Company would experience a significantly adverse effect if &nbsp;these customers were lost and could not be replaced.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>The Company could experience delays in the delivery of its products:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company purchases its products from other vendors and a delay in shipment from these vendors to the Company could cause significant delays in delivery to the Company&#146;s customers. This could result in a decrease in sales orders to the Company.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>A loss of the bank credit agreement could impact future liquidity:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company currently maintains a line of credit with U.S. Bank in the amount of $5 million. A loss of this credit line could have a significantly adverse effect on the liquidity of the Company.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 11</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><I>The limited daily trading volume of the Company&#146;s common stock could make it difficult for investors to purchase additional shares or sell currently held shares in the open market:</I></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The shares of the Company currently trade within the NASDAQ system in the United States and on the Toronto Stock Exchange in Canada. The average daily trading volume of the Company&#146;s common stock is 500 shares within the NASDAQ system and significantly less on the Toronto Stock Exchange. &nbsp;With this limited trading volume investors could find it difficult to purchase or sell the Company&#146;s common stock. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM 2. &nbsp;DESCRIPTION OF PROPERTY</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company&#146;s executive offices are located at 32775 NW Hillcrest, North Plains, Oregon &nbsp;97133. &nbsp;The Company purchased the five acres of land for $350,000 in January 1995 and finished construction for $850,000 of the 40,000 sq.ft. facility (6,000 sq.ft. of office space, 10,000 sq.ft. of manufacturing space, and 24,000 sq.ft. of warehouse space) in October 1995.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The facility provides office space for all of the Company&#146;s executive offices and is used as a distribution center to service the Company&#146;s customer base from northern California to Alaska.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In July 1994, the Company purchased a distribution complex at 9501 West 900 South, Ogden, Utah for $295,000. &nbsp;This 30-acre, 28,500 sq.ft. facility is used to service the Company&#146;s customer base in the Rocky Mountain region.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In October 2000, the Company purchased all of the assets, including land, buildings and equipment of Agrobiotech Inc. (Hillsboro) for total proceeds of $1,530,762. The Company operates its wholly owned subsidiary, Jewett-Cameron Seed Company out of this facility. This facility consists of thirteen plus acres of land, 105,000 square feet of buildings; rolling stock; and, equipment. It is currently used exclusively for seed processing, seed storage and seed brokerage. It is located at 31345 N.W. Beach Road in the town of Hillsboro, Oregon. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In February 2002, the Company purchased the business and certain assets of Greenwood Forest Products, Inc. Jewett-Cameron Lumber Company, a wholly-owned subsidiary of Jewett-Cameron Trading Company Ltd., operates its wholly owned subsidiary Greenwood Products, Inc. out of this facility which is located at 15895 S.W. 72nd Avenue, Suite 200 in Tigard, Oregon. The Company pays a monthly lease payment for this 8,000 square foot facility of $14,000. There are currently twenty-five people employed here.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 12</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM 3. &nbsp;LEGAL PROCEEDINGS</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The &nbsp;Company &nbsp;knows &nbsp;of no material, active &nbsp;or &nbsp;pending &nbsp;legal proceedings &nbsp;against &nbsp;them; nor is the Company &nbsp;involved &nbsp;as &nbsp;a plaintiff in any material proceeding or pending litigation.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company knows of no active or pending proceedings against anyone that might materially adversely affect an interest of the Company.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM 4. &nbsp;SUBMISSION OF MATTERS TO A VOTE OF SECURITY HOLDERS</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>No matters were submitted to a vote of security holders through solicitation or otherwise during the fourth quarter of the fiscal year covered by this report.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=center><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=center><B>PART II</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM 5. &nbsp;MARKET FOR REGISTRANT&#146;S COMMON EQUITY</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><U>AND RELATED STOCKHOLDER MATTERS</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Registrant's common stock is issued in registered form. &nbsp;Computershare Investor Services, Inc. (located in Vancouver, British Columbia, Canada) is the registrar and transfer agent for the common stock.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>On 11/14/02, the shareholders' list for the Registrant's common shares showed 28 registered shareholders and 1,018,562 shares outstanding, including 22 registered holders in the United States holding 1,015,890 shares.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>As of 11/14/02, the Registrant estimates that there are 40 &#147;holders of record&#148; of its common stock resident in the United States holding the above referenced 1,015,890 shares.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>As of 11/14/02, the Registrant estimates there are over 350 total beneficial shareholders of its common stock.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Registrant completed a one-for-five share consolidation in March 1996. &nbsp;All references to per share prices and the number of shares refer to post-consolidation data unless otherwise indicated.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Registrant's common shares trade on the NASDAQ Small Capital stock exchange in the United States, having the trading symbol &quot;JCTCF&quot; and CUSIP# 47733C-20-7. &nbsp;The common stock commenced public trading on NASDAQ in April 1996.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Table No. 1 lists the volume of trading and high, low and closing sales prices on the NASDAQ Small Capital stock exchange for the Registrant's common shares for the last eight fiscal quarters. &nbsp;The price was $8.26 on 11/14/02.</P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000">Page 14</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>There are no restrictions that limit the Registrant&#146;s ability to pay dividends on its common stock. &nbsp;The Registrant has not declared any dividends since incorporation and does not anticipate that it will do so in the foreseeable future. &nbsp;The present policy of the Registrant is to retain future earnings for use in its operations and expansion of its business.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>If dividends were to be paid, Canadian law states that in the case of dividends paid to residents not of Canada, the Canadian tax is withheld by the Registrant, which remits only the net amount to the shareholder. &nbsp;By virtue of Article X of the Tax Convention, the rate of tax on dividends paid to residents of the United States is generally limited to 15% of the gross dividend (or 10% in the case of certain corporate shareholders owning at least 10% of the Registrant&#146;s voting shares). &nbsp;In the absence of the treaty provisions, the rate of Canadian withholding tax imposed on non-residents is 25% of the gross dividend. &nbsp;Stock dividends received by non-residents from the Registrant are taxable by Canada as ordinary dividends.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B><U>ITEM NO. 6. &nbsp;SELECTED FINANCIAL DATA</U></B></P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:12pt; font-size:12pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The selected financial data in Table No. 3 for Fiscal 2002/2001/2000 ended August 31st was derived from the &nbsp;financial statements of the Company which were audited by Davidson &amp; Company, independent Chartered Accountants, as indicated in their report which is included elsewhere in this Annual Report. &nbsp;The selected financial data for Fiscal 1999/1998 was derived from audited financial statements of the Company, not included herein.</P>
