<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Accounts receivable &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6,098,733 &nbsp;6,098,733 &nbsp;1,864,991 &nbsp;1,864,991</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Accounts payable and accrued</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;liabilities &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4,018,760 &nbsp;4,018,760 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;684,891 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;684,891</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>Income taxes</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Income taxes are provided in accordance with SFAS No. 109, &quot;Accounting for Income Taxes&quot;. &nbsp;A deferred tax asset or liability is recorded for all temporary differences between financial and tax reporting and net operating loss carryforwards. &nbsp;Deferred tax expense (benefit) results from the net change during the year of deferred tax assets and liabilities.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 38</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>JEWETT-CAMERON TRADING COMPANY LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>NOTES TO THE CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>(Expressed in U.S. Dollars)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>AUGUST 31, 2002</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:504pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U><BR></U></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>2.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING POLICIES</B> (cont'd...)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>Income taxes</B> (cont&#146;d&#133;)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Deferred tax assets are reduced by a valuation allowance when, in the opinion of management, it is more likely than not that some portion or all of the deferred tax assets will not be realized. &nbsp;Deferred tax assets and liabilities are adjusted for the effects of changes in tax laws and rates on the date of enactment.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>New accounting pronouncements</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In June, 2001, the Financial Accounting Standards Board (&quot;FASB&quot;) approved the issuance of Statement of Financial Accounting Standards (&quot;SFAS&quot;) No. 142, &quot;Goodwill and Other Intangible Assets&quot;. &nbsp;SFAS No. 142 addresses the accounting for all purchased intangible assets, but not the accounting for internally developed intangible assets. &nbsp;Goodwill will no longer be amortized but will be reviewed for impairment in accordance with SFAS No. 142. &nbsp;SFAS No. 142 is effective for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2001. &nbsp;Early adoption is permitted for entities with fiscal years beginning after March 15, 2001.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In July 2001, FASB issued SFAS No. 143, &quot;Accounting for Asset Retirement Obligations&quot; that records the fair value of the liability for closure and removal costs associated with the legal obligations upon retirement or removal of any tangible long-lived assets. &nbsp;The initial recognition of the liability will be capitalized as part of the asset cost and depreciated over its estimated useful life. &nbsp;SFAS 143 is required to be adopted effective January 1, 2003. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In August 2001, FASB issued SFAS No. 144, &quot;Accounting for the Impairment or Disposal of Long-Lived Assets&quot; that supersedes SFAS No.&nbsp;121 &quot;Accounting for the Impairment or Disposal of Long-Lived Assets and for Long-Lived Assets to Be Disposed Of.&quot; &nbsp;SFAS No. 144 is required to be adopted effective January 1, 2002.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In April 2002, FASB issued No. 145, &#147;Rescission of FASB Statements No. 4, 44 and 64, Amendment of FASB Statement No. 13, and Technical Corrections&quot;. &nbsp;SFAS No. 145 eliminates the requirement that gains and losses from the extinguishment of debt be aggregated and, if material, classified as an extraordinary item, net of the related income tax effect and eliminates an inconsistency between the accounting for sale-leaseback transactions and certain lease modifications that have economic effects that are similar to sale-leaseback transactions. Generally, SFAS No. 145 is effective for transactions occurring after May 15, 2002.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In June 2002, the FASB issued SFAS No. 146 &quot;Accounting for Costs Associated with Exit or Disposal Activities&quot; that nullifies Emerging Issues Task Force Issue No. 94-3 (&quot;EITF Issue 94-3&quot;) &quot;Liability Recognition for Certain Employee Termination Benefits and Other Costs to Exit an Activity (Including Certain Costs Incurred in a Restructuring)&quot;. &nbsp;SFAS No. 146 requires that a liability for a cost associated with an exit or disposal activity be recognized when the liability is incurred, whereby EITF Issue 94-3 had recognized the liability at the commitment date to an exit plan. &nbsp;The provisions of this statement are effective for exit or disposal activities that are initiated after December 31, 2002 with earlier application encouraged.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The adoption of these new pronouncements is not expected to have a material effect on the Company's financial position or results of operations.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Page 39</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt; color:#000000" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>JEWETT-CAMERON TRADING COMPANY LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>NOTES TO THE CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>(Expressed in U.S. Dollars)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>AUGUST 31, 2002</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:504pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U><BR></U></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>3.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>BUSINESS COMBINATION AND ACQUISITION</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:504pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>During fiscal 2001, the Company acquired all of the assets, including land, buildings and equipment of Agrobiotech Inc. (Hillsboro) for total proceeds of $1,530,762.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The cost of the acquisition was allocated as follows:</P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Holders of common stock are entitled to one vote for each share held. &nbsp;There are no restrictions that limit the Company's ability to pay dividends on its common stock. &nbsp;The Company has not declared any dividends since incorporation.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36.5pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>Treasury stock</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Treasury stock is recorded at cost. &nbsp;During fiscal 2002 and 2001, the Company repurchased 24,200 and 31,500 shares, respectively, at an aggregate cost of $175,059 and $168,554, respectively.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>During the current year, the Company also cancelled 76,500 common shares (2001 &#150; Nil) with an average cost of $418,983 (2001 - $Nil). &nbsp;The premium paid to acquire these shares over their per share book value in the amount of $289,175 (2001 - $Nil) was recorded as a decrease to retained earnings.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>9.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>STOCK OPTIONS </B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company has a stock option plan under which stock options to purchase securities from the Company can be granted to directors and employees of the Company on terms and conditions acceptable to the regulatory authorities of Canada, notably the Toronto Stock Exchange (&quot;TSX&quot;), the Ontario Securities Commission and the British Columbia Securities Commission. &nbsp;The Company has no formal written stock option plan.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>NOTES TO THE CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>(Expressed in U.S. Dollars)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>AUGUST 31, 2002</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:504pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U><BR></U></P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>9.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36.5pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>STOCK OPTIONS</B> (cont&#146;d&#133;)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>In accordance with regulatory policies stock options for up to 10% of the number of issued and outstanding common shares may be granted from time to time, provided that stock options in favour of any one individual may not exceed 5% of the issued and outstanding common shares. &nbsp;No stock option granted under the stock option program is transferable by the optionee other than by will or the laws of descent and distribution, and each stock option is exercisable during the lifetime of the optionee only by such optionee.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The exercise price of all stock options, granted under the stock option program, must be at least equal to the fair market value (subject to regulated discounts) of such common shares on the date of grant.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Proceeds received by the Company from exercise of stock options are credited to capital stock.</P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Risk-free interest rate &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3% &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Expected life of the options &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2 years &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Expected volatility &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;41.62% &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Expected dividend yield &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;--------------------------------------------------------------</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Black-Scholes option pricing model was developed for estimating the fair value of traded options that have no vesting restrictions and are fully transferable. &nbsp;Because option valuation models require the use of subjective assumptions, changes in these assumptions can materially affect the fair value of the options, and the Company's options do not have the characteristics of traded options, so the option valuation models do not necessarily provide a reliable measure of the fair value of its options.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>10.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>EMPLOYEE STOCK OWNERSHIP PLAN</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company sponsors an employee stock ownership plan (&quot;ESOP&quot;) that covers all U.S. employees who are employed by the Company on August 31 of each year and who have at least one thousand hours with the Company in the twelve months preceding that date. &nbsp;The ESOP grants to participants in the plan certain ownership rights in, but not possession of, the common stock of the Company held by the Trustee of the Plan. &nbsp;Shares of common stock are allocated annually to participants in the ESOP pursuant to a prescribed formula. &nbsp;The Company accounts for its ESOP in accordance with SOP-93-6 (Employers' Accounting for Employee Stock Ownership Plans). &nbsp;The Company records compensation expense equal to the market price of the shares acquired on the open market. &nbsp;Any dividends on allocated ESOP shares are recorded as a reduction of retained earnings. &nbsp;ESOP compensation expense was $155,051, $82,530 and $79,141, for 2002, 2001 and 2000, respectively. &nbsp;The ESOP shares as of August&nbsp;31 were as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-------------------------------------------------------------------</P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>AUGUST 31, 2002</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:504pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><U><BR></U></P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>11.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:36.5pt; width:540pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>CONTINGENT LIABILITIES AND COMMITMENTS</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-12.7pt; width:490.8pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>a)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:490.8pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>At August 31, 2002 and 2001, the Company had an un-utilized line-of-credit of approximately $2,000,000 and $4,500,000, respectively.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-49.2pt; width:490.8pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-49.2pt; width:490.8pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:49.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-13.5pt; width:490.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>b)</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:490.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>On March 1, 2002 the Company entered into an agreement with Greenwood Forest Products, Inc. (&#147;Greenwood&#148;) to acquire certain assets of Greenwood. &nbsp;The assets being acquired consist of nearly $7 million of inventory, purchased in seven installments over the next two years for a price equal to the seller&#146;s cost plus 2%; furnishings, equipment and supplies for $260,000 payable at closing (paid); and a license to use all of the intangible assets of the seller for a five year term, with an option to purchase the intangible assets for a nominal amount of $1,000, payable at closing (paid). &nbsp;To date, the Company has made the first two installments for the purchase of inventory in the amount of $1,799,828. &nbsp;Subsequent to year end, the Company made the third installment for the purchase of inventory (Note&nbsp;15).</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:490.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Greenwood is in the business of processing and distribution of industrial wood and other specialty building products, principally to original equipment manufacturers. </P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-49.2pt; width:490.8pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-49.2pt; width:490.8pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:49.2pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-49.2pt; width:490.8pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-10pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>12.</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>SEGMENTED INFORMATION</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>The Company has four principal operating segments: the sales of building materials and industrial wood products to home improvements centres and original equipment manufacturers in the United States; the sale of pneumatic air tools and industrial clamps in the United States; and the processing and sales of agricultural seeds in the United States. &nbsp;These operating segments were determined based on the nature of the products offered. &nbsp;Operating segments are defined as components of an enterprise about which separate financial information is available that is evaluated regularly in deciding how to allocate resources and in assessing performance. &nbsp;The Company evaluates performance based on several factors, of which the primary financial measure is business segment income before taxes. &nbsp;The following tables show the operations of the Company's reportable segments.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>

<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><B>CONCENTRATIONS OF CREDIT RISK</B></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:540pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0pt; width:503.5pt; line-height:10pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify>Financial instruments that potentially subject the Company to concentrations of credit risk consist primarily of cash and cash equivalents and accounts receivable. &nbsp;The Company places its cash and cash equivalents with high quality financial institutions and limits the amount of credit exposure with any one institution. &nbsp;The Company has concentrations of credit risk with respect to accounts receivable as large amounts of its accounts receivable are concentrated geographically in the United States amongst a small number of customers. &nbsp;At August 31, 2002, one customer totalling $825,722 and at August 31, 2001 two customers totalling $419,817 and $1,056,600, respectively, accounted for accounts receivable greater than 10% of total accounts receivable. &nbsp;The Company controls credit risk through credit approvals, credit limits, and monitoring procedures. &nbsp;The Company performs credit evaluations of its commercial customers but generally does not require collateral to support accounts receivable.</P>
<P style="margin-left:36pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36.5pt; padding-top:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-36.5pt; width:503.5pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000" align=justify><BR></P>
